    var dataTransform = function(data){
        var allData = {};
        var text = "";

        for(var k=0 ; k< data.length ; k++){
            if(!jQuery.isEmptyObject(data[k])){
                $.extend( allData, data[k] );
            }
        }

        var keys = Object.keys(allData).sort();
        
        for(var k = 0 ; k < keys.length ; k++){
          text += (allData[keys[k]] || "")
        }
        console.log(text.length);

        text = text.replace(/\r/g, "");
        text = text.replace(/\t/g, "");
        //text = text.split(/\n/g);
        var temp = "";
        for (var k = 0 ; k < text.length ; k ++){
            if(text[k] == "\n"){
                temp+="\n[SPLITTER_BCKSP]";
            }else if(k!=0 && k%30==0){
                temp+="[SPLITTER_BCKSP]"+text[k];
            }else{
                temp+=text[k];
            }
        }
        text = temp.split("[SPLITTER_BCKSP]");  
        return text;
    };
